   /*--Toggles emergency Drawers 1 and 2 on 'X' Click--*/
      $(document).ready(function() {
        $(".emergency__toggle").click(function() {
          $(".emergency-box-area").slideToggle("fast");
        });

        $(".emergency-two__toggle").click(function() {
          $(".emergency-message-2-area").slideToggle("fast");
        });
        
        $(".emergency-three__toggle").click(function() {
          $(".emergency-message-3-area").slideToggle("fast");
        });  

      });
  </script>
